SAMPLE      UF4 sample of a thickness of 92.13+-0.46 ug/cm2       23164001   39 
           was produced through vacuum evaporation on gold        23164001   40

           calibration; produced by vacuum evaporation on a       23164001   44 
           polyimide backing covered by Au (53.+-0.6 ug/cm2)      23164001   45

DETECTOR   (FISCH)  Twin Frisch-grid ionization chamber using     23164001   76 
           both analogue and digital data acquisition techniques. 23164001   77 
           Twin Frisch Grid Ionization Chamber (TFGIC) with two   23164001   78 
           anodes, two grids and a common cathode. As counting    23164001   79 
           gas P10 (90% Argon, 10% Methane) is used in continuous 23164001   80 
           flow 0.1 l/min, at gas pressure 1.05*10**5 Pa.         23164001   81 
METHOD      Energies and angles of both fragments are measured    23164001   82 
           using the double E method, conservation of energy and  23164001   83 
           momentum is assumed to calculate FF masses.            23164001   84 
ASSUMED    (ASSUM1,92-U-235(N,F),PRE,AKE,LF+HF)                   23164001   85 
            235U(nth,f) <TKE>=170.5+/-0.5 MeV for pulse height    23164001   86 
            defect correction following Hambsch et al.(1995).     23164001   87 
           (ASSUM2,92-U-235(N,F),PRE,AP,HF)                       23164001   88 
            235U(nth,f) <AH>=139.6+/-0.1 for pulse height defect  23164001   89 
            correction following Hambsch et al.(1995).            23164001   90 
ANALYSIS   '2E method' was applied.                               23164001   91 
           The final data analysis was mainly done for the digital23164001   92 
           system, due to its superiority over the analogue data. 23164001   93 
CORRECTION  Energy-loss correction.                               23164001   94 
            Pulse-height defect correction.                       23164001   95 
            Correction for neutron emission by parameterization of23164001   96 
            NU dependence from mass A as:                         23164001   97 
            NU234(A)=1/2*(NU235(A)+NU233(A),                      23164001   98 
            where NU for U235 and U233 thermal neutron fission are23164001   99 
            used - see REL-REF of C.Wahl;                         23164001  100 
            for NU dependence from TKE - formula (5) in           23164001  101 
            J,PR/C,93,034603,2016 was used;                       23164001  102 
            linear interpolation to the neutron data from REL-REF 23164001  103 
            of D.Mather+ was done to estimate the total neutron   23164001  104 
            emission as a function of incident-neutron energy.    23164001  105 
ADD-RES    -The measured two-dimensional mass yield and TKE       23164001  106 
           distribution have been described in terms of fission   23164001  107 
           modes. The yield of the standard 1 (S1) mode shows     23164001  108 
           fluctuations in the threshold of the fission cross     23164001  109 
           section due to the influence of the resonance and      23164001  110 
           levels off at about 20% yield for higher incident      23164001  111 
           neutron energies. The S2 mode shows the respective     23164001  112 
           opposite behavior. The mean TKE of both modes          23164001  113 
           decreases with En. The decrease in mean TKE overrules  23164001  114 
           the increase in S1 yield, so the mean TKE is dropping  23164001  115 
           as a function of En above 2.5 MeV.                     23164001  116 
           - Post-neutron-emission kinetic energy of HF as a      23164001  117 
           function of post-neutron-emission mass for En=5MeV is  23164001  118 
           presented for two methods (see SUBENTs 011 -AV, 012-HV)23164001  119 
           on fig.5a of Phys.Rev.,C86(2012)054601                 23164001  120 
           - The pre-neutron-emission and post-neutron-emission   23164001  121 
           mass yields for En=5MeV for HF and LF are presented    23164001  122 
           for two methods (see SUBENTs 011 -AV, 012-HV) on       23164001  123 
           fig.6 of J,PR/C,86,054601,2012.                        23164001  124 
           - TKE and mean pre-neutron-emission mass as function of23164001  125 
           total NU for AV method ( see SUBENT 011) for EN=5MeV   23164001  126 
           are presented on fig.9a of Phys.Rev.,C86(2012)054601   23164001  127
